***

##### `asString` <a name="asString" id="cdktn.Token.asString"></a>

```typescript
import { Token } from 'cdktn'

Token.asString(value: any, options?: EncodingOptions)
```

Return a reversible string representation of this token.

If the Token is initialized with a literal, the stringified value of the
literal is returned. Otherwise, a special quoted string representation
of the Token is returned that can be embedded into other strings.

Strings with quoted Tokens in them can be restored back into
complex values with the Tokens restored by calling `resolve()`
on the string.

###### `value`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="value" id="cdktn.Token.asString.parameter.value"></a>

- *Type:* any

***

###### `options`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="options" id="cdktn.Token.asString.parameter.options"></a>

- *Type:* <a href="#cdktn.EncodingOptions">EncodingOptions</a>

***

##### `asStringMap` <a name="asStringMap" id="cdktn.Token.asStringMap"></a>

```typescript
import { Token } from 'cdktn'

Token.asStringMap(value: any, options?: EncodingOptions)
```

Return a reversible map representation of this token.

###### `value`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="value" id="cdktn.Token.asStringMap.parameter.value"></a>

- *Type:* any

***

###### `options`<sup>Optional</sup> <a name="options" id="cdktn.Token.asStringMap.parameter.options"></a>

- *Type:* <a href="#cdktn.EncodingOptions">EncodingOptions</a>

***

##### `isUnresolved` <a name="isUnresolved" id="cdktn.Token.isUnresolved"></a>

```typescript
import { Token } from 'cdktn'

Token.isUnresolved(obj: any)
```

Returns true if obj represents an unresolved value.

One of these must be true:

- `obj` is an IResolvable
- `obj` is a string containing at least one encoded `IResolvable`
- `obj` is either an encoded number or list

This does NOT recurse into lists or objects to see if they
containing resolvables.

###### `obj`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="obj" id="cdktn.Token.isUnresolved.parameter.obj"></a>

- *Type:* any

The object to test.

***

##### `nullValue` <a name="nullValue" id="cdktn.Token.nullValue"></a>

```typescript
import { Token } from 'cdktn'

Token.nullValue()
```

Return a Token containing a `null` value.

Note: This is different than `undefined`, `nil`, `None` or similar
as it will end up in the Terraform config and can be used to explicitly
not set an attribute (which is sometimes required by Terraform providers)

#### Constants <a name="Constants" id="Constants"></a>

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Token.property.ANY_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE">ANY\_MAP\_TOKEN\_VALUE</a></code> | <code>string</code> | Any map token representation. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Token.property.NUMBER_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE">NUMBER\_MAP\_TOKEN\_VALUE</a></code> | <code>number</code> | Number Map token value representation. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Token.property.STRING_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE">STRING\_MAP\_TOKEN\_VALUE</a></code> | <code>string</code> | String Map token value representation. |

***

##### `ANY_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="ANY_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE" id="cdktn.Token.property.ANY_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE"></a>

```typescript
public readonly ANY_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE: string;
```

- *Type:* string

Any map token representation.

***

##### `NUMBER_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="NUMBER_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE" id="cdktn.Token.property.NUMBER_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE"></a>

```typescript
public readonly NUMBER_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE: number;
```

- *Type:* number

Number Map token value representation.

***

##### `STRING_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="STRING_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE" id="cdktn.Token.property.STRING_MAP_TOKEN_VALUE"></a>

```typescript

```

- *Type:* string

String Map token value representation.

### Tokenization <a name="Tokenization" id="cdktn.Tokenization"></a>

Less oft-needed functions to manipulate Tokens.

#### Initializers <a name="Initializers" id="cdktn.Tokenization.Initializer"></a>

```typescript
import { Tokenization } from 'cdktn'

new Tokenization()
```

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |

***

#### Static Functions <a name="Static Functions" id="Static Functions"></a>

| **Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.isResolvable">isResolvable</a></code> | Return whether the given object is an IResolvable object. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.resolve">resolve</a></code> | Resolves an object by evaluating all tokens and removing any undefined or empty objects or arrays. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverse">reverse</a></code> | Reverse any value into Resolvables, if possible. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverseList">reverseList</a></code> | Un-encode a Tokenized value from a list. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverseMap">reverseMap</a></code> | Un-encode a Tokenized value from a map. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverseNumber">reverseNumber</a></code> | Un-encode a Tokenized value from a number. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverseNumberList">reverseNumberList</a></code> | Un-encode a Tokenized value from a list. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.reverseString">reverseString</a></code> | Un-encode a string potentially containing encoded tokens. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.Tokenization.stringifyNumber">stringifyNumber</a></code> | Stringify a number directly or lazily if it's a Token. |

***

##### `isResolvable` <a name="isResolvable" id="cdktn.Tokenization.isResolvable"></a>

```typescript
import { Tokenization } from 'cdktn'

Tokenization.isResolvable(obj: any)
```

Return whether the given object is an IResolvable object.

This is different from Token.isUnresolved() which will also check for
encoded Tokens, whereas this method will only do a type check on the given
object.

###### `obj`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="obj" id="cdktn.Tokenization.isResolvable.parameter.obj"></a>

- *Type:* any

***

##### `resolve` <a name="resolve" id="cdktn.Tokenization.resolve"></a>

```typescript
import { Tokenization } from 'cdktn'

Tokenization.resolve(obj: any, options: ResolveOptions)
```

Resolves an object by evaluating all tokens and removing any undefined or empty objects or arrays.

Values can only be primitives, arrays or tokens. Other objects (i.e. with methods) will be rejected.

###### `obj`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="obj" id="cdktn.Tokenization.resolve.parameter.obj"></a>

- *Type:* any

The object to resolve.

***

###### `options`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="options" id="cdktn.Tokenization.resolve.parameter.options"></a>

- *Type:* <a href="#cdktn.ResolveOptions">ResolveOptions</a>

Prefix key path components for diagnostics.

***

##### `reverse` <a name="reverse" id="cdktn.Tokenization.reverse"></a>

```typescript
import { Tokenization } from 'cdktn'

Tokenization.reverse(x: any)
```

Reverse any value into Resolvables, if possible.

###### `x`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="x" id="cdktn.Tokenization.reverse.parameter.x"></a>

- *Type:* any

***

##### `reverseList` <a name="reverseList" id="cdktn.Tokenization.reverseList"></a>

```typescript
import { Tokenization } from 'cdktn'

Tokenization.reverseList(l: string[])
```

Un-encode a Tokenized value from a list.

###### `l`<sup>Required</sup> <a name="l" id="cdktn.Tokenization.reverseList.parameter.l"></a>

- *Type:* string\[]

##### `stringifyNumber` <a name="stringifyNumber" id="cdktn.Tokenization.stringifyNumber"></a>

```typescript

```

### TokenizedStringFragments <a name="TokenizedStringFragments" id="cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments"></a>

Fragments of a concatenated string containing stringified Tokens.

#### Initializers <a name="Initializers" id="cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.Initializer"></a>

```typescript
import { TokenizedStringFragments } from 'cdktn'

new TokenizedStringFragments()
```

| **Name** | **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |

***

#### Methods <a name="Methods" id="Methods"></a>

| **Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.addEscape">addEscape</a></code> | *No description.* |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.addIntrinsic">addIntrinsic</a></code> | Adds an intrinsic fragment. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.addLiteral">addLiteral</a></code> | Adds a literal fragment. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.addToken">addToken</a></code> | Adds a token fragment. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.concat">concat</a></code> | *No description.* |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.join">join</a></code> | Combine the string fragments using the given joiner. |
| <code><a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.mapTokens">mapTokens</a></code> | Apply a transformation function to all tokens in the string. |

***

##### `concat` <a name="concat" id="cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments.concat"></a>


- *Type:* <a href="#cdktn.TokenizedStringFragments">TokenizedStringFragments</a>
